================================================================================

--- REQUEST:
POST /sap/bc/adt/programs/programs/zbds_wm085?_action=UNLOCK&lockHandle=693093157A967F7E9F87828A1BCF76FB8705C846 HTTP/1.1
sap-adt-request-id: 12d48589f80547aeae83cc6029ad38c6
User-Agent: Eclipse/4.37.0.v20250905-0730 (win32; x86_64; Java 21.0.8) ADT/3.54.0 (devedition)
X-sap-adt-profiling: server-time

--- RESPONSE:
HTTP/1.1 200 OK
~server_protocol: HTTP/1.1
X-sap-adt-profiling: server-time=2216

--- REQUEST:

If-None-Match: 202604141618050004
